// Ad Block detection code per ticket AST-440
ga('provide', 'adblockTracker', function(tracker) {
    // If we have already detected an ad blocker, then short-circuit
    if (adsBlocked) {
        sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension4 = "true";
        return;
    }
    var ad = document.createElement('ins');
    ad.className = 'AdSense';
    ad.style.display = 'block';
    ad.style.position = 'absolute';
    ad.style.top = '-1px';
    ad.style.height = '1px';
    document.body.appendChild(ad);
    adsBlocked = ad.clientHeight >0 ? adsBlocked : true; // If height < 1 then we assume a blocker
    document.body.removeChild(ad);
    sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension4 = adsBlocked ? "true" : "false"; // GA requires a string value
});
ga('provide', 'getPageType', function(tracker) {
    var path = window.location.pathname;

    if (path === "/") {
        // 'pathname' will not return any query string or hash, so this should work for all site types
        sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension6 = "home";
        return;
    }
    if (path.indexOf("/gallery/") >-1) {
        sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension6 = "gallery";
        return;
    }
    if (path.indexOf("/weather") === 0) {
        // Includes all subsections of /weather, per request
        sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension6 = "weather";
        return;
    }
    if (path.indexOf("/traffic") === 0) {
        // Includes all subsections of /traffic, per request
        sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension6 = "traffic";
        return;
    }
    if (path.indexOf("/watch") === 0) {
        // The News3 version of the Watch page uses this Head component instead of type_news_v3/head/v3
        sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension6 = "watch";
        return;
    }

    // All other sections should report as simply "section"
    sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension6 = "section";
});

function extractDomainFromUrl(fullUrl) {
    if (typeof fullUrl === 'string' && fullUrl != '') {
        var domainString = '';
        try {
            if (fullUrl.indexOf('://') >-1) {
                fullUrl = fullUrl.split('://')[1];
            }
            fullUrl = fullUrl.split('/')[0];
            var domainArray = fullUrl.split('.');
            var domainPosition = domainArray.length - 2;
            var domainString = domainArray[domainPosition].toLowerCase();
        } catch(excp) {
        }
        return domainString;
    } else {
        return '';
    }
}
